***пособие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бие</a> (6681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>According to Vasmer, ultimately a univerbation corresponding to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sebé</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пособник.html>посо́бник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">posóbnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подсобный.html>подсо́бный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podsóbnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posóbije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пособие.html>посо́бий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>allowance, benefit, pension, dole; gratuity</li>
<li>handbook, manual, tutorial, textbook</li></ol>

***посол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посо́л</a> (4528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">посълъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">posŭlŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*posъlъ</i>. Probably originally deverbal from the ancestor of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poslátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or alternatively from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*po-</i> + the deverbal form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъlati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посо́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>послы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посло́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>legate; ambassador</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poslátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>слать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посох.html>по́сох</a> (7026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">посохъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">posoxŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соха.html>соха́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">soxá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wooden plough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, q. v.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посох.html>по́сох</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pósox</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посох.html>по́соха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посох.html>по́сохи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посох.html>по́сохов</a></b>)

***поспавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поспать.html>поспа́вший</a> (7441)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспать.html>поспа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pospávšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспать.html>поспа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pospátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***поспевать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поспевать.html>поспева́ть</a> (10701)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспеть.html>поспе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pospétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-вать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспевать.html>поспева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pospevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспеть.html>поспе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen</li>
<li>to make it, to be on time, etc.</li></ol>

***поспеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поспеть.html>поспе́ть</a> (12620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспеть.html>поспе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pospétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспевать.html>поспева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen</li>
<li>to make it, to be on time, etc.</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спешить.html>спеши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spešítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поспорить.html>поспо́рить</a> (9694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спорить.html>спо́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spóritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспорить.html>поспо́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pospóritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спорить.html>спо́рить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dispute, to argue (for some time)</li>
<li>to discuss, to debate (for some time)</li>
<li>to bet, to wager</li></ol>

***посрамить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посрамить.html>посрами́ть</a> (20706)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">срами́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sramítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посрамить.html>посрами́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posramítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">посрамля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shame, to disgrace, to dishonor</li>
<li>to expose, to debunk</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:посредник.html>посре́дник</a> (10147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посредник.html>посре́дник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posrédnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посредник.html>посре́дника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посредник.html>посре́дники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посредник.html>посре́дников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">посре́дница</b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посреднический.html>посре́днический</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mediator, intermediary, negotiator</li>
<li>agent, broker, middleman</li>
<li>umpire</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">посредница</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">posrednica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посредничество.html>посре́дничество</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">posrédničestvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посредственность.html>посре́дственность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">posrédstvennostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посредник.html>посре́дник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">posrédnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-eskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посреднический.html>посре́днический</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">posrédničeskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> intermediary, mediator, mediation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:посреднический.html>посре́днические</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>posrédničeskije</b> uslúgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>mediation</b> services</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
